\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00876}00876\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\`{}y2`)."{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00877}00877\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00878}00878\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{raise}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classValueError}{ValueError}}(msg)\ \textcolor{keyword}{from}\ e}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00879}00879\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{raise}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00880}00880\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00881}00881\ \ \ \ \ n\_classes\ =\ confusion.shape[0]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00882}00882\ \ \ \ \ sum0\ =\ np.sum(confusion,\ axis=0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00883}00883\ \ \ \ \ sum1\ =\ np.sum(confusion,\ axis=1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00884}00884\ \ \ \ \ expected\ =\ np.outer(sum0,\ sum1)\ /\ np.sum(sum0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00885}00885\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00886}00886\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ weights\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{is}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{None}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00887}00887\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ w\_mat\ =\ np.ones([n\_classes,\ n\_classes],\ dtype=int)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00888}00888\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ w\_mat.flat[::\ n\_classes\ +\ 1]\ =\ 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00889}00889\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}:\ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ "{}linear"{}\ or\ "{}quadratic"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00890}00890\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ w\_mat\ =\ np.zeros([n\_classes,\ n\_classes],\ dtype=int)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00891}00891\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ w\_mat\ +=\ np.arange(n\_classes)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00892}00892\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ weights\ ==\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}linear"{}}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00893}00893\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ w\_mat\ =\ np.abs(w\_mat\ -\/\ w\_mat.T)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00894}00894\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00895}00895\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ w\_mat\ =\ (w\_mat\ -\/\ w\_mat.T)\ **\ 2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00896}00896\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00897}00897\ \ \ \ \ k\ =\ np.sum(w\_mat\ *\ confusion)\ /\ np.sum(w\_mat\ *\ expected)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00898}00898\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ float(1\ -\/\ k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00899}00899\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l00900}00900\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01114}01114\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ measure\ of\ the\ quality\ of\ binary\ and\ multiclass\ classifications.\ It\ takes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01115}01115\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ into\ account\ true\ and\ false\ positives\ and\ negatives\ and\ is\ generally}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01116}01116\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ regarded\ as\ a\ balanced\ measure\ which\ can\ be\ used\ even\ if\ the\ classes\ are\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01117}01117\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ very\ different\ sizes.\ The\ MCC\ is\ in\ essence\ a\ correlation\ coefficient\ value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01118}01118\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ between\ -\/1\ and\ +1.\ A\ coefficient\ of\ +1\ represents\ a\ perfect\ prediction,\ 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01119}01119\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ an\ average\ random\ prediction\ and\ -\/1\ an\ inverse\ prediction.\ \ The\ statistic}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01184}01184\ \ \ \ \ C\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceconfusion__matrix}{confusion\_matrix}}(y\_true,\ y\_pred,\ sample\_weight=sample\_weight)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01185}01185\ \ \ \ \ t\_sum\ =\ C.sum(axis=1,\ dtype=np.float64)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01186}01186\ \ \ \ \ p\_sum\ =\ C.sum(axis=0,\ dtype=np.float64)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01187}01187\ \ \ \ \ n\_correct\ =\ np.trace(C,\ dtype=np.float64)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01188}01188\ \ \ \ \ n\_samples\ =\ p\_sum.sum()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01189}01189\ \ \ \ \ cov\_ytyp\ =\ n\_correct\ *\ n\_samples\ -\/\ np.dot(t\_sum,\ p\_sum)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01190}01190\ \ \ \ \ cov\_ypyp\ =\ n\_samples**2\ -\/\ np.dot(p\_sum,\ p\_sum)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01191}01191\ \ \ \ \ cov\_ytyt\ =\ n\_samples**2\ -\/\ np.dot(t\_sum,\ t\_sum)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01192}01192\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01193}01193\ \ \ \ \ cov\_ypyp\_ytyt\ =\ cov\_ypyp\ *\ cov\_ytyt}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01194}01194\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ cov\_ypyp\_ytyt\ ==\ 0:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01195}01195\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ 0.0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01196}01196\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01197}01197\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ float(cov\_ytyp\ /\ np.sqrt(cov\_ypyp\_ytyt))}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01313}01313\ ):}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01314}01314\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}"{}"{}Compute\ the\ F1\ score,\ also\ known\ as\ balanced\ F-\/score\ or\ F-\/measure.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01315}01315\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01316}01316\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ The\ F1\ score\ can\ be\ interpreted\ as\ a\ harmonic\ mean\ of\ the\ precision\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01317}01317\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ recall,\ where\ an\ F1\ score\ reaches\ its\ best\ value\ at\ 1\ and\ worst\ score\ at\ 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01318}01318\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ The\ relative\ contribution\ of\ precision\ and\ recall\ to\ the\ F1\ score\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01319}01319\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ equal.\ The\ formula\ for\ the\ F1\ score\ is:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01320}01320\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01321}01321\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ ..\ math::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01322}01322\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)text\{F1\}\ =\ \(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)frac\{2\ *\ \(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)text\{TP\}\}\{2\ *\ \(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)text\{TP\}\ +\ \(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)text\{FP\}\ +\ \(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)text\{FN\}\}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01323}01323\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01324}01324\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Where\ :math:\`{}\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)text\{TP\}\`{}\ is\ the\ number\ of\ true\ positives,\ :math:\`{}\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)text\{FN\}\`{}\ is\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01325}01325\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ number\ of\ false\ negatives,\ and\ :math:\`{}\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)text\{FP\}\`{}\ is\ the\ number\ of\ false\ positives.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01326}01326\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ F1\ is\ by\ default}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01327}01327\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ calculated\ as\ 0.0\ when\ there\ are\ no\ true\ positives,\ false\ negatives,\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01328}01328\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ false\ positives.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01329}01329\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01330}01330\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Support\ beyond\ :term:\`{}binary\`{}\ targets\ is\ achieved\ by\ treating\ :term:\`{}multiclass\`{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01331}01331\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ and\ :term:\`{}multilabel\`{}\ data\ as\ a\ collection\ of\ binary\ problems,\ one\ for\ each}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01332}01332\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ label.\ For\ the\ :term:\`{}binary\`{}\ case,\ setting\ \`{}average='binary'\`{}\ will\ return}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01333}01333\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ F1\ score\ for\ \`{}pos\_label\`{}.\ If\ \`{}average\`{}\ is\ not\ \`{}'binary'\`{},\ \`{}pos\_label\`{}\ is\ ignored}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01334}01334\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ and\ F1\ score\ for\ both\ classes\ are\ computed,\ then\ averaged\ or\ both\ returned\ (when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01335}01335\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \`{}average=None\`{}).\ Similarly,\ for\ :term:\`{}multiclass\`{}\ and\ :term:\`{}multilabel\`{}\ targets,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01336}01336\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ F1\ score\ for\ all\ \`{}labels\`{}\ are\ either\ returned\ or\ averaged\ depending\ on\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01337}01337\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \`{}average\`{}\ parameter.\ Use\ \`{}labels\`{}\ specify\ the\ set\ of\ labels\ to\ calculate\ F1\ score}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01338}01338\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ for.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01339}01339\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01340}01340\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Read\ more\ in\ the\ :ref:\`{}User\ Guide\ <precision\_recall\_f\_measure\_metrics>\`{}.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01511}01511\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ reaching\ its\ optimal\ value\ at\ 1\ and\ its\ worst\ value\ at\ 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01512}01512\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01513}01513\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ The\ \`{}beta\`{}\ parameter\ represents\ the\ ratio\ of\ recall\ importance\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01514}01514\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ precision\ importance.\ \`{}beta\ >\ 1\`{}\ gives\ more\ weight\ to\ recall,\ while}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01515}01515\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \`{}beta\ <\ 1\`{}\ favors\ precision.\ For\ example,\ \`{}beta\ =\ 2\`{}\ makes\ recall\ twice}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01516}01516\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ as\ important\ as\ precision,\ while\ \`{}beta\ =\ 0.5\`{}\ does\ the\ opposite.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01517}01517\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Asymptotically,\ \`{}beta\ -\/>\ +inf\`{}\ considers\ only\ recall,\ and\ \`{}beta\ -\/>\ 0\`{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01518}01518\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ only\ precision.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l01519}01519\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l02570}02570\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ intuitively\ the\ ability\ of\ the\ classifier\ to\ find\ all\ the\ positive\ samples.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l03267}03267\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ always\ negative\ (since\ the\ signs\ disagree),\ implying\ \`{}\`{}1\ -\/\ margin\`{}\`{}\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__classification_8py_source_l03268}03268\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ always\ greater\ than\ 1.\ \ The\ cumulated\ hinge\ loss\ is\ therefore\ an\ upper}}
